-- 清空现有楼层数据
DELETE FROM floor;

-- 为每个广场分配楼层：必须包含B1-F3(23-26)，可向上/下扩展
INSERT INTO floor (Name, Description, PlazaId, FloorItemId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(p.Name, ' - ', d.Label) AS Name,
    CONCAT(d.Label, '层') AS Description,
    p.Id AS PlazaId,
    d.Id AS FloorItemId,
    CONCAT(p.Code, '_', d.Value) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime
FROM plaza p
JOIN dictionaryitem d ON d.Id BETWEEN 
    CASE   -- 随机向下扩展0-3层
        WHEN RAND() < 0.33 THEN 20  -- 包含B4
        WHEN RAND() < 0.66 THEN 21  -- 包含B3-B4  
        ELSE 22                     -- 包含B2-B4
    END 
    AND 
    CASE   -- 随机向上扩展0-3层
        WHEN RAND() < 0.33 THEN 26  -- 仅B1-F3
        WHEN RAND() < 0.66 THEN 27  -- 到F4
        WHEN RAND() < 0.85 THEN 28  -- 到F5
        ELSE 29                     -- 到F6
    END
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
  AND d.Id BETWEEN 20 AND 29
  AND d.DictionaryId = 5
ORDER BY p.Id, d.Id;

-- 验证结果：确保每个广场都有B1-F3(23-26)
SELECT 
    p.Name AS 广场名称,
    p.Code AS 广场代码,
    COUNT(f.Id) AS 楼层数量,
    MIN(d.Label) AS 起始楼层,
    MAX(d.Label) AS 结束楼层,
    GROUP_CONCAT(d.Label ORDER BY d.Id) AS 完整连续楼层,
    CASE 
    
        WHEN SUM(CASE WHEN d.Id = 23 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0 
         AND SUM(CASE WHEN d.Id = 24 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0
         AND SUM(CASE WHEN d.Id = 25 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0
         AND SUM(CASE WHEN d.Id = 26 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0
        THEN '✅ 包含B1-F3'
        ELSE '❌ 缺少必要楼层'
    END AS 检查状态
FROM plaza p
JOIN floor f ON p.Id = f.PlazaId
JOIN dictionaryitem d ON f.FloorItemId = d.Id
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0 AND f.IsDeleted = 0
GROUP BY p.Id, p.Name, p.Code
ORDER BY p.Id;


-- 为 SuperAdmin 角色创建菜单访问权限
INSERT INTO `plazashop`.`permission` 
(`name`, `description`, `roleid`, `code`, `isdeleted`, `createtime`)
SELECT 
    CONCAT('访问_', m.`name`), 
    CONCAT('允许访问菜单: ', m.`name`), 
    1, -- SuperAdmin 的角色 ID
    CONCAT('PERM_', m.`code`), 
    0, 
    NOW()
FROM `plazashop`.`sysmenu` m
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM `plazashop`.`permission` p 
    WHERE p.`roleid` = 1 AND p.`code` = CONCAT('PERM_', m.`code`)
);

INSERT INTO `plazashop`.`menupermission`
(`menuid`, `permissionid`, `code`, `isdeleted`, `createtime`)
SELECT 
    m.`id`, 
    p.`id`, 
    CONCAT('MENU_PERM_', m.`code`), 
    0, 
    NOW()
FROM `plazashop`.`sysmenu` m
JOIN `plazashop`.`permission` p ON p.`code` = CONCAT('PERM_', m.`code`) AND p.`roleid` = 1
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM `plazashop`.`menupermission` mp 
    WHERE mp.`menuid` = m.`id` AND mp.`permissionid` = p.`id`
);

-- =====================================================
-- 3. 设备数据 (Device) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE device;

INSERT INTO device (Name, Location, DeviceStatusItemId, LastMaintenanceDate, DeviceTypeId, FloorId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN dt.Id = 1 THEN '温度传感器' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 2 THEN '湿度传感器' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 3 THEN '空气质量监测' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 4 THEN '电力监测' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 5 THEN '客流统计' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 6 THEN '安防监控' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 7 THEN '照明控制' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 8 THEN '电梯监控' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 9 THEN '停车引导' 
            WHEN dt.Id = 10 THEN '紧急报警' 
        END, 
        '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.Id, dt.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 2, '0') 
    ) AS Name,
    CONCAT(
        d.Label,
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.25 THEN 'A区'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'B区'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.75 THEN 'C区'
            ELSE 'D区'
        END,
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, 2, '0'), '号'
    ) AS Location,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 4) + 1, 5, 6, 7, 8) AS DeviceStatusItemId,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 60) DAY) AS LastMaintenanceDate,
    dt.Id AS DeviceTypeId,
    f.Id AS FloorId,
    CONCAT(
        SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_',
        CASE 
            WHEN d.Label LIKE '地下%' THEN CONCAT('B', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 3, 1))
            WHEN d.Label LIKE '负%' THEN CONCAT('B', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 2, 1))
            ELSE CONCAT('F', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 1, 1))
        END,
        '_', dt.Code, '_',
        LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.Id, dt.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 2, '0')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM floor f
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
JOIN dictionaryitem d ON f.FloorItemId = d.Id
JOIN (SELECT 1 AS Id, 'DT001' AS Code UNION SELECT 2, 'DT002' UNION SELECT 3, 'DT003' UNION SELECT 4, 'DT004' UNION SELECT 5, 'DT005' UNION SELECT 6, 'DT006' UNION SELECT 7, 'DT007' UNION SELECT 8, 'DT008' UNION SELECT 9, 'DT009' UNION SELECT 10, 'DT010') dt ON 1=1
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0 AND f.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.7
ORDER BY f.Id, dt.Id;

-- 4. 真实品牌商铺数据 (Store) - 使用真实品牌名称
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE store;

-- 创建品牌数据临时表
CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE temp_real_brands (
    brand_name VARCHAR(100),
    store_type_id INT,
    category VARCHAR(20),
    description TEXT
);

('阿尔卑斯室内滑雪训练基地', 5, 'entertainment', '室内滑雪训练'),
('祥云极速国际卡丁车馆', 5, 'entertainment', '卡丁车赛车馆');

INSERT INTO store (Name, ImageUrl, SwiperImageUrl, Location, BusinessHours, Contact, Description, Rating, IsOperating, StoreTypeId, FloorId, UserId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    b.brand_name AS Name,
    COALESCE(CONCAT('images/logo.png'), '') AS ImageUrl,
    CONCAT('images/store/storelogo.png') AS SwiperImageUrl, -- 修复了此处语法
    CONCAT(
        d.Label,
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.2 THEN 'A区'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.4 THEN 'B区'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'C区'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.8 THEN 'D区'
            ELSE 'E区'
        END,
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 50) + 1, 2, '0'), '号铺'
    ) AS Location,
    CASE 
        WHEN b.category IN ('restaurant', 'entertainment') THEN 
            CASE 
                WHEN RAND() < 0.4 THEN '10:00-22:00'
                WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN '09:30-21:30'
                ELSE '10:00-02:00'
            END
        ELSE 
            CASE 
                WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN '10:00-22:00'
                WHEN RAND() < 0.8 THEN '09:30-21:30'
                ELSE '10:00-21:00'
            END
    END AS BusinessHours,
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'BJ%' THEN '010'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SH%' THEN '021'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'TJ%' THEN '022'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'CQ%' THEN '023'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GD%' THEN '020'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'JS%' THEN '025'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'ZJ%' THEN '0571'
            WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SD%' THEN '0531'
            ELSE '400'
        END,
        '-',
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 90000000) + 10000000, 8, '0')
    ) AS Contact,
    b.description AS Description,
    ROUND(3.8 + RAND() * 1.2, 1) AS Rating,
    1 AS IsOperating,
    b.store_type_id AS StoreTypeId,
    f.Id AS FloorId,
    (SELECT Id FROM USER ORDER BY RAND() LIMIT 1) AS UserId,
    CONCAT(
        SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_',
        CASE 
            WHEN d.Label LIKE '地下%' THEN CONCAT('B', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 3, 1))
            WHEN d.Label LIKE '负%' THEN CONCAT('B', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 2, 1))
            ELSE CONCAT('F', SUBSTRING(d.Label, 1, 1))
        END,
        '_', b.category, '_',
        LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.Id, b.brand_name ORDER BY RAND()), 3, '0')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM floor f
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
JOIN dictionaryitem d ON f.FloorItemId = d.Id
CROSS JOIN temp_real_brands b
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0 
  AND f.IsDeleted = 0
  AND d.Id BETWEEN 23 AND 28
  -- 确保同一商城内同一品牌不重复
  AND NOT EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 
      FROM store s2 
      JOIN floor f2 ON s2.FloorId = f2.Id 
      WHERE f2.PlazaId = f.PlazaId 
        AND s2.Name = b.brand_name
  )
  -- 每个商城随机选择12-20个品牌
  AND RAND() < 0.55  -- 55%概率选中，确保每个商城有适量品牌
ORDER BY f.Id, RAND();

-- 清理临时表
DROP TEMPORARY TABLE temp_real_brands;


-- =====================================================
-- 5. 商品类型数据 (ProductType) - 基于真实品牌动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE producttype;

INSERT INTO producttype (Name, StoreId, ProductTypeUnitItemId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT DISTINCT
    CASE 
        WHEN st.Id = 1 THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, '女装', '男装', '童装', '鞋履', '配饰', '包包')
        WHEN st.Id = 2 THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1, '美妆', '日用品', '数码', '食品', '家居')
        WHEN st.Id = 3 THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 4) + 1, '玩具', '童装', '童鞋', '母婴用品')
        WHEN st.Id = 4 THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1, '中餐', '西餐', '火锅', '茶饮', '小吃')
        WHEN st.Id = 5 THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 3) + 1, '电影票', '游戏币', '会员服务')
        ELSE '其他商品'
    END AS Name,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CASE 
        WHEN st.Id IN (1, 3) THEN 55  -- 件
        WHEN st.Id = 2 THEN 55       -- 件
        WHEN st.Id = 4 THEN 52       -- 份
        WHEN st.Id = 5 THEN 51       -- 个
        ELSE 55
    END AS ProductTypeUnitItemId,
    CONCAT(
        SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_',
        st.Code, '_',
        MD5(CONCAT(s.Id, FLOOR(RAND() * 1000)))
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN storetype st ON s.StoreTypeId = st.Id
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
ORDER BY s.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 6. 商品数据 (Product) - 基于真实店铺动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE product;

INSERT INTO product (Name, ImageUrl, Description, ProductTypeId, StoreId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%优衣库%' THEN CONCAT('优衣库', 
                CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'U系列' ELSE '设计师合作款' END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%ZARA%' THEN CONCAT('ZARA', 
                CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN '新款' ELSE '经典款' END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%H&M%' THEN CONCAT('H&M', 
                CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'Conscious系列' ELSE 'Studio系列' END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%无印良品%' THEN CONCAT('无印良品', 
                CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN '基础款' ELSE '限定款' END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%星巴克%' THEN CONCAT('星巴克', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '拿铁'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '美式'
                    ELSE '星冰乐'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%麦当劳%' THEN CONCAT('麦当劳', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '巨无霸'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '麦辣鸡腿堡'
                    ELSE '麦乐鸡'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%肯德基%' THEN CONCAT('肯德基', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '吮指原味鸡'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '香辣鸡腿堡'
                    ELSE '新奥尔良烤翅'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%海底捞%' THEN CONCAT('海底捞', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '招牌虾滑'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '毛肚'
                    ELSE '牛肉'
                end)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%屈臣氏%' THEN CONCAT('屈臣氏', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '面膜'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '洗面奶'
                    ELSE '防晒霜'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%丝芙兰%' THEN CONCAT('丝芙兰', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '口红'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '粉底'
                    ELSE '眼影'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%耐克%' THEN CONCAT('耐克', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN 'Air Force 1'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'Air Max'
                    ELSE 'Jordan'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%阿迪达斯%' THEN CONCAT('阿迪达斯', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN 'Stan Smith'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'Superstar'
                    ELSE 'Ultraboost'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN CONCAT('苹果', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN 'iPhone'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'iPad'
                    ELSE 'MacBook'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%华为%' THEN CONCAT('华为', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN 'P系列'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'Mate系列'
                    ELSE 'nova系列'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%小米%' THEN CONCAT('小米', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '数字系列'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN 'Redmi系列'
                    ELSE 'MIX系列'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%超市%' THEN CONCAT(
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '新鲜'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '进口'
                    ELSE '有机'
                END,
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '水果'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '蔬菜'
                    ELSE '零食'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%影院%' THEN CONCAT('电影票_', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '2D'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '3D'
                    ELSE 'IMAX'
                END)
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%书店%' THEN CONCAT(
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '畅销'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '经典'
                    ELSE '新书'
                END,
                '图书')
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%儿童%' THEN CONCAT('儿童', 
                CASE 
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '玩具'
                    WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '服装'
                    ELSE '用品'
                END)
            ELSE CONCAT(s.Name, ' ', pt.Name)
        END,
        ' ', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY s.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 3, '0')
    ) AS Name,
    '' AS ImageUrl,
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%优衣库%' THEN '优衣库官方正品，简约时尚设计，舒适面料'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%ZARA%' THEN 'ZARA当季新品，紧跟时尚潮流，优质面料'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%H&M%' THEN 'H&M时尚单品，环保材质，潮流设计'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%无印良品%' THEN '无印良品简约设计，天然材质，品质生活'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%星巴克%' THEN '星巴克精选咖啡豆，专业烘焙，醇香口感'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%麦当劳%' THEN '麦当劳经典美味，新鲜食材，品质保证'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%肯德基%' THEN '肯德基秘制配方，香脆可口，回味无穷'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%海底捞%' THEN '海底捞精选食材，秘制锅底，服务至上'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%屈臣氏%' THEN '屈臣氏正品保障，专业护肤，美丽加倍'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%丝芙兰%' THEN '丝芙兰国际大牌，专业美妆，正品保证'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%耐克%' THEN '耐克官方正品，专业运动科技，舒适体验'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%阿迪达斯%' THEN '阿迪达斯经典设计，运动科技，品质保证'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN '苹果官方正品，创新科技，卓越体验'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%华为%' THEN '华为官方正品，科技创新，智慧生活'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%小米%' THEN '小米高性价比，智能科技，年轻时尚'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%超市%' THEN '超市精选商品，新鲜直达，品质优选'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%影院%' THEN '影院观影体验，震撼视听，沉浸享受'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%书店%' THEN '书店精选图书，正版保证，知识海洋'
            WHEN s.Name LIKE '%儿童%' THEN '儿童专业品牌，安全材质，益智成长'
            ELSE CONCAT('优质', pt.Name, '，官方正品保证')
        END
    ) AS Description,
    pt.Id AS ProductTypeId,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(
        SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_',
        pt.Code, '_',
        LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY pt.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 3, '0')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM producttype pt
JOIN store s ON pt.StoreId = s.Id
JOIN storetype st ON s.StoreTypeId = st.Id
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.8  -- 80%概率生成商品
ORDER BY s.Id, pt.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 7. 商品SKU数据 (ProductSku) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE productsku;

INSERT INTO productsku (Name, SkuCode, BarCode, ImageUrl, Price, CostPrice, MarketPrice, StockQuantity, Sales, Weight, IsEnabled, ProductId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(p.Name, ' - ', 
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.2 THEN '标准版'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.4 THEN '豪华版'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '旗舰版'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.8 THEN '专业版'
            ELSE '基础版'
        END,
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.25 THEN ' - 红色'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN ' - 蓝色'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.75 THEN ' - 黑色'
            ELSE ' - 白色'
        END,
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.33 THEN ' - S'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.66 THEN ' - M'
            ELSE ' - L'
        END
    ) AS Name,
    CONCAT(
        'SKU_', 
        LPAD(p.Id, 4, '0'), '_',
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 900000) + 100000, 6, '0'), '_',
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 99) + 1, 2, '0')
    ) AS SkuCode,
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.33 THEN '69'
            WHEN RAND() < 0.66 THEN '87'
            ELSE '97'
        END,
        FLOOR(RAND() * 9000000000000) + 1000000000000
    ) AS BarCode,
    '' AS ImageUrl,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%优衣库%' THEN ROUND(79 + RAND() * 400, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%ZARA%' THEN ROUND(199 + RAND() * 800, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%星巴克%' THEN ROUND(25 + RAND() * 100, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN ROUND(3999 + RAND() * 8000, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%耐克%' THEN ROUND(299 + RAND() * 1200, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%超市%' THEN ROUND(5 + RAND() * 200, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%影院%' THEN ROUND(35 + RAND() * 100, 0)
        ELSE ROUND(99 + RAND() * 900, 0)
    END AS Price,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%优衣库%' THEN ROUND(39 + RAND() * 200, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%ZARA%' THEN ROUND(99 + RAND() * 400, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%星巴克%' THEN ROUND(12 + RAND() * 50, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN ROUND(1999 + RAND() * 4000, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%耐克%' THEN ROUND(149 + RAND() * 600, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%超市%' THEN ROUND(2 + RAND() * 100, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%影院%' THEN ROUND(18 + RAND() * 50, 0)
        ELSE ROUND(49 + RAND() * 450, 0)
    END AS CostPrice,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%优衣库%' THEN ROUND(99 + RAND() * 500, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%ZARA%' THEN ROUND(249 + RAND() * 1000, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%星巴克%' THEN ROUND(35 + RAND() * 120, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN ROUND(4999 + RAND() * 10000, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%耐克%' THEN ROUND(399 + RAND() * 1500, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%超市%' THEN ROUND(8 + RAND() * 250, 0)
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%影院%' THEN ROUND(45 + RAND() * 120, 0)
        ELSE ROUND(129 + RAND() * 1100, 0)
    END AS MarketPrice,
    FLOOR(RAND() * 500) + 50 AS StockQuantity,
    FLOOR(RAND() * 100) AS Sales,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Name LIKE '%苹果%' THEN ROUND(0.3 + RAND() * 0.7, 2)
        ELSE ROUND(0.1 + RAND() * 0.4, 2)
    END AS Weight,
    1 AS IsEnabled,
    p.Id AS ProductId,
    CONCAT(
        'SKU_', 
        LPAD(p.Id, 4, '0'), '_',
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 900000) + 100000, 6, '0'), '_',
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 99) + 1, 2, '0')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM product p
JOIN producttype pt ON p.ProductTypeId = pt.Id
JOIN store s ON p.StoreId = s.Id
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.8  -- 80%商品生成SKU
ORDER BY p.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 7. 商品规格 (ProductSpec) - 基于商品动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE productspec;

INSERT INTO productspec (Name, Sort, GoodsId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    '版本' AS Name,
    1 AS Sort,
    p.Id AS GoodsId,
    CONCAT('SPEC_VER_', LPAD(p.Id, 4, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM product p
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    '颜色' AS Name,
    2 AS Sort,
    p.Id AS GoodsId,
    CONCAT('SPEC_COLOR_', LPAD(p.Id, 4, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM product p
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    '尺寸' AS Name,
    3 AS Sort,
    p.Id AS GoodsId,
    CONCAT('SPEC_SIZE_', LPAD(p.Id, 4, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM product p
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
ORDER BY GoodsId, Sort;

-- =====================================================
-- 8. 商品规格值 (ProductSpecValue) - 基于规格动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE productspecvalue;

INSERT INTO productspecvalue (SpecId, Value, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    ps.Id AS SpecId,
    CASE 
        WHEN ps.Name = '版本' THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 4) + 1, '标准版', '专业版', '旗舰版', '限量版')
        WHEN ps.Name = '颜色' THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 8) + 1, '红色', '蓝色', '黑色', '白色', '金色', '银色', '绿色', '紫色')
        WHEN ps.Name = '尺寸' THEN ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, 'XS', 'S', 'M', 'L', 'XL', 'XXL')
    END AS Value,
    CONCAT(
        CASE 
            WHEN ps.Name = '版本' THEN 'VAL_VER'
            WHEN ps.Name = '颜色' THEN 'VAL_COL'
            WHEN ps.Name = '尺寸' THEN 'VAL_SIZ'
        END,
        '_',
        LPAD(ps.GoodsId, 4, '0'),
        '_',
        LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY ps.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 2, '0')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM productspec ps
WHERE ps.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.8  -- 80%的规格有值
ORDER BY ps.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 9. 商品SKU与规格关联 (ProductSkuSpecValue) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE productskuspecvalue;

INSERT INTO productskuspecvalue (ProductSkuId, ProductSpecValueId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    ps.Id AS ProductSkuId,
    psv.Id AS ProductSpecValueId,
    CONCAT('PSSV_', ps.Code, '_', psv.Code) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM productsku ps
JOIN product p ON ps.ProductId = p.Id
JOIN productspec pspec ON pspec.GoodsId = p.Id
JOIN productspecvalue psv ON psv.SpecId = pspec.Id
WHERE ps.IsDeleted = 0
  AND psv.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.6  -- 60%概率建立关联
ORDER BY ps.Id, psv.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 10. 员工角色数据 (EmployeeRole) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE employeerole;

INSERT INTO employeerole (Name, Description, StoreId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    '店长' AS Name,
    '全面负责店铺运营管理' AS Description,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_', s.Code, '_ROLE_01') AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    '副店长' AS Name,
    '协助店长管理店铺日常运营' AS Description,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_', s.Code, '_ROLE_02') AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    '收银员' AS Name,
    '负责收银和客户服务' AS Description,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_', s.Code, '_ROLE_03') AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    '导购员' AS Name,
    '负责商品销售和客户服务' AS Description,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_', s.Code, '_ROLE_04') AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0;

-- =====================================================
-- 14. 员工数据 (Employee) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE employee;

INSERT INTO employee (Name, Gender, Wage, CommissionRate, Contact, HireDate, EmployeeRoleId, StoreId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN CONCAT(
            ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '张', '王', '李', '赵', '刘', '陈', '杨', '黄', '周', '吴', '徐', '孙', '胡', '朱', '高', '林', '何', '郭', '马', '罗'),
            ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '伟', '芳', '娜', '秀英', '敏', '静', '丽', '强', '磊', '军', '洋', '勇', '艳', '杰', '娟', '涛', '明', '超', '秀兰', '霞')
        )
        ELSE CONCAT(
            ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '张', '王', '李', '赵', '刘', '陈', '杨', '黄', '周', '吴', '徐', '孙', '胡', '朱', '高', '林', '何', '郭', '马', '罗'),
            ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '云', '天', '宇', '文', '思', '雅', '涵', '晨', '轩', '瑞', '博', '浩', '然', '峰', '鹏', '成', '龙', '雪', '美', '佳')
        )
    END AS Name,
    CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 1 ELSE 2 END AS Gender,
    CASE 
        WHEN er.Name = '店长' THEN ROUND(8000 + RAND() * 7000, 0)
        WHEN er.Name = '副店长' THEN ROUND(6000 + RAND() * 5000, 0)
        WHEN er.Name = '收银员' THEN ROUND(4000 + RAND() * 3000, 0)
        ELSE ROUND(3500 + RAND() * 3500, 0)
    END AS Wage,
    CASE 
        WHEN er.Name = '店长' THEN 0.05
        WHEN er.Name = '副店长' THEN 0.04
        WHEN er.Name = '收银员' THEN 0.02
        ELSE 0.03
    END AS CommissionRate,
    CONCAT('1', LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 9000000000) + 1000000000, 10, '0')) AS Contact,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 365) + 30 DAY) AS HireDate,
    er.Id AS EmployeeRoleId,
    s.Id AS StoreId,
    CONCAT(SUBSTRING_INDEX(p.Code, '_', 1), '_', s.Code, '_EMP_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY s.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 3, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM store s
JOIN employeerole er ON s.Id = er.StoreId
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.8  -- 80%店铺有员工
ORDER BY s.Id, er.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 11. 地址数据 (Address) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE address;

INSERT INTO address (UserId, Name, Phone, Province, City, County, Detail, Label, IsDefault, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    u.Id AS UserId,
    IFNULL(
        CASE 
            WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN CONCAT(
                ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '张', '王', '李', '赵', '刘', '陈', '杨', '黄', '周', '吴', '徐', '孙', '胡', '朱', '高', '林', '何', '郭', '马', '罗'),
                ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '先生', '女士', '小姐', '老师', '医生', '工程师', '经理', '老板', '老师', '教授')
            )
            ELSE CONCAT(
                ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '张', '王', '李', '赵', '刘', '陈', '杨', '黄', '周', '吴', '徐', '孙', '胡', '朱', '高', '林', '何', '郭', '马', '罗'),
                ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '家', '府', '宅', '居', '舍', '苑', '庭', '院', '公馆', '别墅')
            )
        END,
        CONCAT('用户', FLOOR(RAND() * 9999) + 1)
    ) AS Name,
    CONCAT('1', LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 9000000000) + 1000000000, 10, '0')) AS Phone,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'BJ%' THEN '北京市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SH%' THEN '上海市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'TJ%' THEN '天津市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'CQ%' THEN '重庆市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GD%' THEN '广东省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'JS%' THEN '江苏省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'ZJ%' THEN '浙江省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SD%' THEN '山东省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HEN%' THEN '河南省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HB%' THEN '湖北省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HN%' THEN '湖南省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SC%' THEN '四川省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'FJ%' THEN '福建省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'AH%' THEN '安徽省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'JX%' THEN '江西省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GX%' THEN '广西壮族自治区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'YN%' THEN '云南省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GZ%' THEN '贵州省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SX%' THEN '山西省'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HB_YU%' THEN '河北省'
        ELSE '北京市'
    END AS Province,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'BJ%' THEN '北京市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SH%' THEN '上海市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'TJ%' THEN '天津市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'CQ%' THEN '重庆市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GD%' THEN '广州市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'JS%' THEN '南京市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'ZJ%' THEN '杭州市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SD%' THEN '济南市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HEN%' THEN '郑州市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HB%' THEN '武汉市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HN%' THEN '长沙市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SC%' THEN '成都市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'FJ%' THEN '福州市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'AH%' THEN '合肥市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'JX%' THEN '南昌市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GX%' THEN '南宁市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'YN%' THEN '昆明市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'GZ%' THEN '贵阳市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'SX%' THEN '太原市'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE 'HB_YU%' THEN '石家庄市'
        ELSE '北京市'
    END AS City,
    CASE 
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_CHAOYANG%' THEN '朝阳区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_HAIDIAN%' THEN '海淀区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_XICHENG%' THEN '西城区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_DONGCHENG%' THEN '东城区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_FENGTAI%' THEN '丰台区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_SHIJINGSHAN%' THEN '石景山区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_TONGZHOU%' THEN '通州区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_CHANGPING%' THEN '昌平区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_DAXING%' THEN '大兴区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_FANGSHAN%' THEN '房山区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_MENTOUGOU%' THEN '门头沟区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_PINGGU%' THEN '平谷区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_HUAIROU%' THEN '怀柔区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_MIYUN%' THEN '密云区'
        WHEN p.Code LIKE '%_YANQING%' THEN '延庆区'
        ELSE '朝阳区'
    END AS County,
    CONCAT(
        ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1, '幸福', '阳光', '和谐', '美好', '温馨'),
        ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1, '家园', '小区', '花园', '公寓', '社区'),
        FLOOR(RAND() * 20) + 1, '号楼',
        FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1, '单元',
        FLOOR(RAND() * 1000) + 1, '室'
    ) AS Detail,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 4) + 1, '家', '公司', '学校', '其他') AS Label,
    CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsDefault,
    CONCAT('ADDR_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY u.Id, RAND()), 6, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM USER u
JOIN plaza p ON 1=1
WHERE u.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.7  -- 70%用户有地址
ORDER BY u.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 12. 停车场区域数据 (ParkingArea) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE parkingarea;

INSERT INTO parkingarea (Name, FloorId, ParkingAreaItemId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(
        ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, 'A区', 'B区', 'C区', 'D区', 'E区', 'F区'),
        '停车场'
    ) AS Name,
    f.Id AS FloorId,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, 14, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19) AS ParkingAreaItemId,
    CONCAT('PA_', p.Code, '_', f.Code, '_', 
        ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, 'A', 'B', 'C', 'D', 'E', 'F')
    ) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM floor f
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
JOIN dictionaryitem d ON f.FloorItemId = d.Id
WHERE f.IsDeleted = 0 
  AND d.Label IN ('F1', 'B1', 'B2', 'B3', 'B4');

-- =====================================================
-- 14. 停车位数据 (ParkingSpot) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE parkingspot;

INSERT INTO parkingspot (Name, ParkingSpotItemId, ParkingAreaId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(
        pa.Name, '_',
        LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY pa.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 3, '0'), '号车位'
    ) AS Name,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 3) + 1, 11, 12, 13) AS ParkingSpotItemId,  -- 随机状态：空闲/占用/维护
    pa.Id AS ParkingAreaId,
    CONCAT('PS_', pa.Code, '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY pa.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 4, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM parkingarea pa
CROSS JOIN (
    SELECT 1 UNION ALL SELECT 2 UNION ALL SELECT 3 UNION ALL SELECT 4 UNION ALL 
    SELECT 5 UNION ALL SELECT 6 UNION ALL SELECT 7 UNION ALL SELECT 8 UNION ALL 
    SELECT 9 UNION ALL SELECT 10 UNION ALL SELECT 11 UNION ALL SELECT 12 UNION ALL
    SELECT 13 UNION ALL SELECT 14 UNION ALL SELECT 15 UNION ALL SELECT 16 UNION ALL
    SELECT 17 UNION ALL SELECT 18 UNION ALL SELECT 19 UNION ALL SELECT 20 UNION ALL
    SELECT 21 UNION ALL SELECT 22 UNION ALL SELECT 23 UNION ALL SELECT 24 UNION ALL
    SELECT 25 UNION ALL SELECT 26 UNION ALL SELECT 27 UNION ALL SELECT 28 UNION ALL
    SELECT 29 UNION ALL SELECT 30 UNION ALL SELECT 31 UNION ALL SELECT 32 UNION ALL
    SELECT 33 UNION ALL SELECT 34 UNION ALL SELECT 35 UNION ALL SELECT 36 UNION ALL
    SELECT 37 UNION ALL SELECT 38 UNION ALL SELECT 39 UNION ALL SELECT 40 UNION ALL
    SELECT 41 UNION ALL SELECT 42 UNION ALL SELECT 43 UNION ALL SELECT 44 UNION ALL
    SELECT 45 UNION ALL SELECT 46 UNION ALL SELECT 47 UNION ALL SELECT 48 UNION ALL
    SELECT 49 UNION ALL SELECT 50
) AS spots
WHERE pa.IsDeleted = 0
ORDER BY pa.Id, RAND();

-- =====================================================
-- 15. 设备数据记录 (DeviceData) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE devicedata;

INSERT INTO devicedata (DeviceId, Value, DeviceDataUnitItemId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    d.Id AS DeviceId,
    CASE 
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%温度%' THEN ROUND(15 + RAND() * 20, 1)
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%湿度%' THEN ROUND(30 + RAND() * 40, 1)
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%空气质量%' THEN ROUND(20 + RAND() * 80, 0)
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%电力%' THEN ROUND(100 + RAND() * 900, 1)
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%客流%' THEN FLOOR(RAND() * 1000)
        ELSE ROUND(RAND() * 100, 1)
    END AS Value,
    CASE 
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%温度%' THEN 1
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%湿度%' THEN 2
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%空气质量%' THEN 3
        WHEN d.Name LIKE '%电力%' THEN 4
        ELSE 1
    END AS DeviceDataUnitItemId,
    CONCAT('DATA_', d.Code, '_', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d%H%i%s'), LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 1000), 3, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM device d
WHERE d.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.7  -- 70%设备有数据
ORDER BY d.Id;

-- =====================================================
-- 完整数据验证查询
-- =====================================================
SELECT '=== 数据初始化完成 ===' AS 状态;

SELECT '广场统计' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM plaza WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '楼层统计' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM floor WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM devicetype
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM device WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '商铺类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM storetype
UNION ALL
SELECT '商铺数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM store WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '商品类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM producttype
UNION ALL
SELECT '商品数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM product WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '员工角色' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM employeerole WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '员工数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM employee WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '地址数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM address WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '停车区域' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM parkingarea WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '停车位' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM parkingspot WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备数据' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM devicedata WHERE IsDeleted = 0;

-- 查看商铺分布详情
SELECT 
    p.Name AS 广场名称,
    st.Name AS 商铺类型,
    COUNT(*) AS 商铺数量,
    GROUP_CONCAT(s.Name ORDER BY s.Name SEPARATOR ', ') AS 商铺列表
FROM store s
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
JOIN storetype st ON s.StoreTypeId = st.Id
WHERE s.IsDeleted = 0
GROUP BY p.Id, st.Id
ORDER BY p.Name, st.Name;

-- =====================================================
-- 16. 订单数据 (Orders) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE `order`;

INSERT INTO `order`
    (TotalAmount, DeliveryType, PickUpDate, OrderStatuItemId,
     ShippingAddress, StoreId, CustomerId, Code,
     IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT
    0                                     AS TotalAmount,
    FLOOR(RAND()*2)                       AS DeliveryType,
    IF(FLOOR(RAND()*2) = 0, NULL, NOW())  AS PickUpDate,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND()*8)+1,
        75,76,77,78,79,80,81,82)        AS OrderStatuItemId,
    CONCAT('地址_',p.Name,'_',f.Name,'_',s.Name) AS ShippingAddress,
    s.Id                                  AS StoreId,
    u.Id                                  AS CustomerId,
    CONCAT('ORDER_',p.Code,'_',s.Code,'_',
           LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.Id,s.Id ORDER BY RAND()),4,'0')) AS Code,
    0                                     AS IsDeleted,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND()*365) DAY) AS CreateTime,
    CASE WHEN RAND()<0.7 THEN NOW() ELSE NULL END   AS UpdateTime
FROM user u
JOIN plaza p ON 1=1
JOIN floor f ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
JOIN store s ON s.FloorId = f.Id
WHERE u.IsDeleted = 0
  AND p.IsDeleted = 0
  AND f.IsDeleted = 0
  AND s.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.3
ORDER BY u.Id, p.Id, s.Id, RAND();

-- =====================================================
-- 17. 订单详情数据 (OrderDetail) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE orderitem;

INSERT INTO orderitem (OrderId, ProductSkuId, Quantity, UnitPrice, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    o.Id AS OrderId,
    ps.Id AS ProductSkuId,
    FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 AS Quantity,
    ps.price AS UnitPrice,
    CONCAT('OD', o.Id, '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY o.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 2, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    o.CreateTime,
    o.UpdateTime
FROM `order` o
JOIN product p ON p.StoreId = o.StoreId
JOIN productsku ps ON ps.ProductId = p.Id
WHERE p.IsDeleted = 0
  AND ps.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.8  -- 80%的订单有详情
ORDER BY o.Id, RAND();

-- 更新订单总金额
UPDATE `order` o 
SET TotalAmount = (
    SELECT SUM(Quantity * UnitPrice) 
    FROM orderitem od 
    WHERE od.OrderId = o.Id AND od.IsDeleted = 0
)
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM orderitem od 
    WHERE od.OrderId = o.Id AND od.IsDeleted = 0
);

-- =====================================================
-- 18. 支付记录数据 (PaymentRecord) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE paymentrecord;

INSERT INTO paymentrecord (OrderId, PaymentMethodItemId, Amount, PaystatuItemId, TransactionId, Code, IsDeleted, PaymentTime, CreateTime, UpdateTime, UserId)
SELECT 
    o.Id AS OrderId,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 6) + 1, 39, 40, 41, 42, 43, 44) AS PaymentMethodItemId,
    o.TotalAmount AS Amount,
    ELT(FLOOR(RAND() * 4) + 1, 30, 32, 33, 34) AS PaystatuItemId, -- 待支付、成功、失败、已退款
    CONCAT('TXN', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d%H%i%s'), LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY o.Id, RAND()), 6, '0')) AS TransactionId,
    CONCAT('PY', o.Id) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    CASE 
        WHEN o.OrderStatuItemId IN (79, 80, 82) THEN DATE_ADD(o.CreateTime, INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 24) + 1 HOUR)
        ELSE o.CreateTime
    END AS PaymentTime,
    o.CreateTime,
    CASE 
        WHEN o.OrderStatuItemId IN (79, 80, 82) THEN DATE_ADD(o.CreateTime, INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 24) + 1 HOUR)
        ELSE NULL 
    END AS UpdateTime,
    o.CustomerId AS UserId
FROM `order` o
WHERE o.TotalAmount > 0
  AND RAND() < 0.9;  -- 90%的订单有支付记录

-- =====================================================
-- 19. 评价数据 (Review) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE review;
-- 
-- INSERT INTO review (ReviewRatingItemId, Content,ImageUrl, OrderItemId, UserId, Code, IsDeleted, UpdateTime)
-- SELECT 
--     FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 AS ReviewRatingItemId,
--     CASE 
--         WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 1 THEN '非常差，不推荐！'
--         WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 2 THEN '一般般，有待改进'
--         WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 3 THEN '还不错，可以接受'
--         WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 4 THEN '很好，值得推荐'
--         ELSE '非常好，超出预期！'
--     END AS Content,
--     '' AS ImageUrl
--     oi.Id AS OrderItemId,
--     o.CustomerId AS UserId,
--     CONCAT('RV', oi.Id) AS Code,
--     0 AS IsDeleted,
--     NULL AS UpdateTime
-- FROM `order` o
-- JOIN orderitem oi ON o.Id = oi.OrderId
-- WHERE o.OrderStatuItemId = 79  -- 只给已完成的订单添加评价
--   AND RAND() < 0.6;  -- 60%的完成订单有评价
INSERT INTO review (
    ReviewRatingItemId, 
    Content, 
    OrderItemId, 
    UserId, 
    Code, 
    IsDeleted, 
    UpdateTime,
    ImageUrl
)
SELECT 
    FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 AS ReviewRatingItemId,
    CASE 
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 1 THEN '非常差，不推荐！'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 2 THEN '一般般，有待改进'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 3 THEN '还不错，可以接受'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 4 THEN '很好，值得推荐'
        ELSE '非常好，超出预期！'
    END AS Content,
    oi.Id AS OrderItemId,
    o.CustomerId AS UserId,
    CONCAT('RV', oi.Id) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NULL AS UpdateTime,
    -- 确保 ImageUrl 非空（根据之前的 NOT NULL 约束）
    CONCAT('https://example.com/review/img/', oi.Id, '.jpg') AS ImageUrl
FROM `order` o
INNER JOIN orderitem oi ON o.Id = oi.OrderId
WHERE o.OrderStatuItemId = 79 
  AND RAND() < 0.61364;
-- =====================================================
-- 20. 停车记录数据 (ParkingRecord) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE parkingrecord;

INSERT INTO parkingrecord (PlateNumber, PlateImageUrl, EntryTime, ExitTime, ParkingFee, IsPaid, DeviceId, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    CONCAT(
        CHAR(65 + FLOOR(RAND() * 26)), CHAR(65 + FLOOR(RAND() * 26)), 
        LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 10000), 4, '0'),
        CHAR(65 + FLOOR(RAND() * 26))
    ) AS PlateNumber,
    CONCAT('images/plates/', UUID(), '.jpg') AS PlateImageUrl,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY) AS EntryTime,
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN DATE_ADD(DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 8) + 1 HOUR)
        ELSE NULL 
    END AS ExitTime,
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN ROUND((TIMESTAMPDIFF(HOUR, DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY), DATE_ADD(DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 8) + 1 HOUR)) * 2), 2)
        ELSE 0 
    END AS ParkingFee,
    CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS IsPaid,
    FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 AS DeviceId,
    CONCAT('PK', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d'), '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY RAND()), 4, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    NOW() AS CreateTime,
    NULL AS UpdateTime
FROM (SELECT 1 UNION SELECT 2 UNION SELECT 3 UNION SELECT 4 UNION SELECT 5 UNION SELECT 6 UNION SELECT 7 UNION SELECT 8 UNION SELECT 9 UNION SELECT 10) t
WHERE RAND() < 0.8;  -- 80%的记录

-- =====================================================
-- 21. 购物车数据 (Cart) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE shoppingcartitem;

INSERT INTO shoppingcartitem (UserId, ProductSkuId, Quantity, Selected, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    u.Id AS UserId,
    ps.Id AS ProductSkuId,
    FLOOR(RAND() * 3) + 1 AS Quantity,
    CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.8 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Selected,
    CONCAT('CT', u.Id, '_', ps.Id, '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY u.Id ORDER BY RAND()), 2, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 7) + 1 DAY) AS CreateTime,
    NOW() AS UpdateTime
FROM user u
JOIN product p ON 1=1
JOIN productsku ps ON ps.ProductId = p.Id
WHERE u.IsDeleted = 0 AND p.IsDeleted = 0 AND ps.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.2  -- 20%的用户-商品组合有购物车记录
ORDER BY u.Id, ps.Id, RAND();

-- =====================================================
-- 22. 用户反馈数据 (UserFeedback) - 动态生成
-- =====================================================
TRUNCATE TABLE userfeedback;

INSERT INTO userfeedback (UserId, Imageurl, Content, Contact, ReplyContent, ReplyTime, Code, IsDeleted, CreateTime, UpdateTime)
SELECT 
    u.Id AS UserId,
    '' AS ImageUrl,
    CASE 
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 1 THEN '希望增加更多支付方式'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 2 THEN '支付页面偶尔会出现卡顿'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 3 THEN '停车场收费有点贵'
        WHEN FLOOR(RAND() * 5) + 1 = 4 THEN '界面设计很美观，操作很方便'
        ELSE '整体体验不错，继续加油'
    END AS Content,
    CASE WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN CONCAT('user', u.Id, '@example.com') ELSE '' END AS Contact,
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.3 THEN '感谢您的反馈，我们会尽快处理'
        WHEN RAND() < 0.6 THEN '您的建议很有价值，我们会认真考虑'
        ELSE ''
    END AS ReplyContent,
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN DATE_ADD(DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 3) + 1 DAY)
        ELSE NULL 
    END AS ReplyTime,
    CONCAT('FD', u.Id, '_', LPAD(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY u.Id, RAND()), 2, '0')) AS Code,
    0 AS IsDeleted,
    DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY) AS CreateTime,
    CASE 
        WHEN RAND() < 0.7 THEN DATE_ADD(DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 30) + 1 DAY), INTERVAL FLOOR(RAND() * 3) + 1 DAY)
        ELSE NULL 
    END AS UpdateTime
FROM user u
WHERE u.IsDeleted = 0
  AND RAND() < 0.15;  -- 15%的用户有反馈

-- =====================================================
-- 完整数据验证查询（包含新业务表）
-- =====================================================
SELECT '=== 完整业务数据初始化完成 ===' AS 状态;

SELECT '广场统计' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM plaza WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '楼层统计' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM floor WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM devicetype
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM device WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '商铺类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM storetype
UNION ALL
SELECT '商铺数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM store WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '商品类型' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM producttype
UNION ALL
SELECT '商品数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM product WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '员工角色' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM employeerole WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '员工数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM employee WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '地址数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM address WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '停车区域' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM parkingarea WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '停车位' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM parkingspot WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '设备数据' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM devicedata WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '订单数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM `order` WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '订单详情' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM orderitem WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '支付记录' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM paymentrecord WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '评价数量' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM review WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '停车记录' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM parkingrecord WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '购物车' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM shoppingcartitem WHERE IsDeleted = 0
UNION ALL
SELECT '用户反馈' AS 类别, COUNT(*) AS 数量 FROM userfeedback WHERE IsDeleted = 0;

-- 查看订单分布详情
SELECT 
    p.Name AS 广场名称,
    s.Name AS 店铺名称,
    COUNT(*) AS 订单数量,
    SUM(o.TotalAmount) AS 总销售额,
    AVG(o.TotalAmount) AS 平均订单金额
FROM `order` o
JOIN store s ON o.StoreId = s.Id
JOIN floor f ON s.FloorId = f.Id
JOIN plaza p ON f.PlazaId = p.Id
WHERE o.IsDeleted = 0
GROUP BY p.Id, s.Id
ORDER BY p.Name, 订单数量 DESC;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 1;
